The application will process local datasets consisting of image sequences, ground truth bounding box JSON files, and model prediction JSON files (containing bounding boxes, classes, and confidence scores). It provides two core views: a statistics dashboard displaying per-class detection metrics (recall, false positive rate, etc.) and an image-by-image comparison view showing visual overlays of ground truth and predicted bounding boxes with distinct visual indicators for correct detections, false positives, and missed detections. The tool prioritizes intuitive visualization, accurate metric calculation, and seamless local file handling.\n     7→  </overview>\n     8→\n     9→  <technology_stack>\n    10→    <frontend>\n    11→      <framework>Vanilla HTML5, CSS3, JavaScript (ES6+)</framework>\n    12→      <styling>Custom CSS with Flexbox/Grid, optional Bootstrap 5 (via CDN) for responsive layout</styling>\n    13→      <visualization>Chart.js (CDN) for statistical charts, Canvas API for bounding box rendering</visualization>\n    14→      <file_handling>FileReader API for local file processing</file_handling>\n    15→      <routing>Client-side routing with JavaScript (hash-based) for page navigation</routing>\n    16→      <icons>Font Awesome (CDN) for visual indicators (check, cross, dash)</icons>\n    17→    </frontend>\n    18→    <backend>\n    19→      <runtime>Python 3.8+</runtime>\n    20→      <framework>Flask 2.0+</framework>\n    21→      <data_processing>\n    22→        - JSON parsing with built-in json module\n    23→        - Image processing with Pillow (PIL) for thumbnail generation\n    24→        - Metric calculation (recall, precision, FPR) with numpy\n    25→      </data_processing>\n    26→      <cors>Flask-CORS for cross-origin resource sharing</cors>\n    27→      <file_management>Built-in os/pathlib for local file system interaction</file_management>\n    28→    </backend>\n    29→    <communication>\n    30→      <api>RESTful endpoints for data processing and retrieval</api>\n    31→      <data_format>JSON for all data exchange between frontend and backend</data_format>\n    32→      <file_upload>Multipart/form-data for batch file upload (optional) or local file path specification</file_handling>\n    33→    </communication>\n    34→    <dependencies>\n    35→      <python>\n    36→        - flask>=2.0.0\n    37→        - flask-cors>=3.0.10\n    38→        - pillow>=9.0.0\n    39→        - numpy>=1.21.0\n    40→      </python>\n    41→      <frontend_cdn>\n    42→        - Chart.js v4.4.0\n    43→        - Bootstrap 5.3.0 (optional)\n    44→        - Font Awesome 6.4.0\n    45→      </frontend_cdn>\n    46→    </dependencies>\n    47→  </technology_stack>\n    48→\n    49→  <prerequisites>\n    50→    <environment_setup>\n    51→      - Python 3.8+ installed on the system\n    52→      - Flask and required dependencies installed via pip: pip install flask flask-cors pillow numpy\n    53→      - Local dataset organized in a structured directory (images in /images, ground truth JSON in /gt, predictions JSON in /predictions)\n    54→      - Backend code in /app directory with app.py as entry point\n    55→      - Frontend assets (HTML/CSS/JS) in /app/static directory\n    56→      - Template files in /app/templates directory\n    57→      - Environment variables (optional) for dataset path configuration (.env file with DATASET_PATH)\n    58→    </environment_setup>\n    59→    <dataset_format>\n    60→      <image_sequence>\n    61→        - All images in a single directory (JPG/PNG format) with consistent naming convention (e.g., img_001.jpg, img_002.png)\n    62→        - Image dimensions consistent or variable (tool should handle both)\n    63→      </image_sequence>\n    64→      <ground_truth_json>\n    65→        - Single JSON file or per-image JSON files (naming matching images: img_001.json)\n    66→        - Structure: {\n    67→            \"filename\": \"img_001.jpg\",\n    68→            \"width\": 1920,\n    69→            \"height\": 1080,\n    70→            \"annotations\": [\n    71→              {\n    72→                \"class\": \"car\",\n    73→                \"bbox\": [x1, y1, x2, y2]  # pixel coordinates (top-left, bottom-right)\n    74→              },\n    75→              ...\n    76→            ]\n    77→          }\n    78→      </ground_truth_json>\n    79→      <prediction_json>\n    80→        - Single JSON file or per-image JSON files (naming matching images: img_001_pred.json)\n    81→        - Structure: {\n    82→            \"filename\": \"img_001.jpg\",\n    83→            \"width\": 1920,\n    84→            \"height\": 1080,\n    85→            \"predictions\": [\n    86→              {\n    87→                \"class\": \"car\",\n    88→                \"bbox\": [x1, y1, x2, y2],\n    89→                \"score\": 0.95  # confidence score (0-1)\n    90→              },\n    91→              ...\n    92→            ]\n    93→          }\n    94→      </prediction_json>\n    95→    </dataset_format>\n    96→  </prerequisites>\n    97→\n    98→  <core_features>\n    99→    <file_handling>\n   100→      - Local dataset path configuration (input field for directory path)\n   101→      - Validation of dataset structure (check for images, GT JSON, prediction JSON)\n   102→      - Batch parsing of all files in the dataset directory\n   103→      - Error handling for missing files, invalid JSON formats, and mismatched filenames\n   104→      - Thumbnail generation for all images (150x150px, aspect ratio preserved)\n   105→      - Caching of parsed data to avoid reprocessing on page refresh\n   106→    </file_handling>\n   107→\n   108→    <statistics_dashboard>\n   109→      <metrics_calculation>\n   110→        - **Recall (True Positive Rate)**: TP / (TP + FN) per class\n   111→        - **Precision**: TP / (TP + FP) per class\n   112→        - **False Positive Rate (FPR)**: FP / (FP + TN) per class\n   113→        - **F1 Score**: 2 * (Precision * Recall) / (Precision + Recall) per class\n   114→        - **Overall Accuracy**: (TP + TN) / (TP + TN + FP + FN)\n   115→        - **Average Precision (AP)** per class (optional)\n   116→        - **Intersection over Union (IoU)** threshold configuration (default: 0.5) for TP/FP/FN classification\n   117→      </metrics_calculation>\n   118→      <visualization>\n   119→        - Bar charts for per-class recall, precision, FPR\n   120→        - Pie charts for class distribution in ground truth vs predictions\n   121→        - Summary table with all metrics for easy comparison\n   122→        - Sortable and filterable metric table (by class name, metric value)\n   123→        - Export statistics to CSV/JSON format\n   124→        - Interactive tooltips on charts showing exact metric values\n   125→      </visualization>\n   126→      <user_interface>\n   127→        - Dropdown for IoU threshold adjustment (0.3 to 0.9 in 0.1 increments)\n   128→        - Class filter (show/hide specific classes in charts/tables)\n   129→        - Confidence score threshold filter for predictions (0.0 to 1.0 slider)\n   130→        - Reset filters button to restore default settings\n   131→        - Summary card with key overall metrics (total images, total classes, average recall/precision)\n   132→      </user_interface>\n   133→    </statistics_dashboard>\n   134→\n   135→    <image_comparison_view>\n   136→      <left_panel>\n   137→        - Searchable and filterable file list (by filename, class presence)\n   138→        - Image thumbnails alongside filenames (150x150px)\n   139→        - Scrollable list with fixed height (occupies 100% of viewport height)\n   140→        - Highlight active/selected image in the list\n   141→        - Pagination (optional) for large datasets (10/20/50 images per page)\n   142→        - Class filter (show only images containing specific classes)\n   143→        - Status filter (show only images with FP/FN/perfect detections)\n   144→      </left_panel>\n   145→      <right_panel>\n   146→        <image_display>\n   147→          - High-resolution image view (scaled to fit viewport, maintain aspect ratio)\n   148→          - Interactive canvas overlay for bounding boxes\n   149→          - Bounding box styles:\n   150→            - True Positive (TP): Green border (2px), green checkmark (✓) at top-left corner\n   151→            - False Positive (FP): Red border (2px), red cross (✗) at top-left corner\n   152→            - False Negative (FN): Red border (2px), red horizontal dash (—) at top-left corner\n   153→          - Bounding box labels (class name + confidence score for predictions)\n   154→          - Zoom/pan functionality for detailed inspection\n   155→          - Toggle visibility of ground truth/prediction boxes\n   156→          - Toggle visibility of box labels/indicators\n   157→        </image_display>\n   158→        <per_image_statistics>\n   159→          - Summary card for current image (filename, dimensions, total GT boxes, total predicted boxes)\n   160→          - Per-class breakdown table (GT count, predicted count, TP, FP, FN for each class)\n   161→          - IoU values for each matched bounding box (optional tooltip on hover)\n   162→          - Confidence score distribution for predictions on current image\n   163→          - Navigation buttons (previous/next image) for sequential viewing\n   164→        </per_image_statistics>\n   165→      </right_panel>\n   166→    </image_comparison_view>\n   167→\n   168→    <navigation>\n   169→      - Top navigation bar with links to Statistics Dashboard and Image Comparison View\n   170→      - Active page indicator in navigation bar\n   171→      - Breadcrumb navigation for context (current dataset path, current image)\n   172→      - Back to top button for long pages (statistics dashboard)\n   173→      - Responsive navigation (collapsible menu on mobile devices)\n   174→    </navigation>\n   175→\n   176→    <error_handling>\n   177→      - User-friendly error messages for invalid dataset paths\n   178→      - Validation errors for malformed JSON files (line number + error description)\n   179→      - Warning messages for mismatched filenames (GT/prediction JSON without corresponding image)\n   180→      - Loading spinners during data processing/file parsing\n   181→      - Empty state handling (no data loaded, no images to display)\n   182→      - Fallback UI for unsupported image formats\n   183→    </error_handling>\n   184→\n   185→    <accessibility>\n   186→      - Keyboard navigation (Tab/Enter for list selection, arrow keys for image navigation)\n   187→      - Alt text for all images and icons\n   188→      - High contrast mode for bounding boxes (optional toggle)\n   189→      - Screen reader compatible labels for all UI elements\n   190→      - Responsive design for mobile/tablet/desktop viewing\n   191→      - Text size adjustment option (small/medium/large)\n   192→    </accessibility>\n   193→  </core_features>\n   194→\n   195→  <database_schema>\n   196→    <tables>\n   197→      <dataset_metadata>\n   198→        - id (primary key, integer)\n   199→        - path (text, unique)\n   200→        - total_images (integer)\n   201→        - total_classes (integer)\n   202→        - iou_threshold (float, default 0.5)\n   203→        - confidence_threshold (float, default 0.5)\n   204→        - created_at (timestamp)\n   205→        - last_updated (timestamp)\n   206→      </dataset_metadata>\n   207→\n   208→      <image_metadata>\n   209→        - id (primary key, integer)\n   210→        - dataset_id (foreign key to dataset_metadata.id)\n   211→        - filename (text)\n   212→        - width (integer)\n   213→        - height (integer)\n   214→        - thumbnail_path (text)\n   215→        - total_gt_boxes (integer)\n   216→        - total_pred_boxes (integer)\n   217→        - has_fp (boolean)\n   218→        - has_fn (boolean)\n   219→        - is_perfect (boolean)\n   220→      </image_metadata>\n   221→\n   222→      <classes>\n   223→        - id (primary key, integer)\n   224→        - dataset_id (foreign key to dataset_metadata.id)\n   225→        - name (text, unique per dataset)\n   226→        - total_gt_count (integer)\n   227→        - total_pred_count (integer)\n   228→        - tp_count (integer)\n   229→        - fp_count (integer)\n   230→        - fn_count (integer)\n   231→        - recall (float)\n   232→        - precision (float)\n   233→        - fpr (float)\n   234→        - f1_score (float)\n   235→      </classes>\n   236→\n   237→      <bounding_boxes>\n   238→        - id (primary key, integer)\n   239→        - image_id (foreign key to image_metadata.id)\n   240→        - class_id (foreign key to classes.id)\n   241→        - type (text, enum: 'ground_truth', 'prediction')\n   242→        - x1 (float)\n   243→        - y1 (float)\n   244→        - x2 (float)\n   245→        - y2 (float)\n   246→        - confidence (float, null for ground truth)\n   247→        - iou (float, null for unmatched boxes)\n   248→        - classification (text, enum: 'tp', 'fp', 'fn', null for unclassified)\n   249→      </bounding_boxes>\n   250→    </tables>\n   251→    <notes>\n   252→      - Database is SQLite (file-based) for simplicity, stored as dataset_analysis.db\n   253→      - Data is cleared/overwritten when a new dataset is loaded\n   254→      - Indexes on filename, class name, and image_id for faster queries\n   255→    </notes>\n   256→  </database_schema>\n   257→\n   258→  <api_endpoints_summary>\n   259→    <dataset>\n   260→      - POST /api/dataset/load: Load and parse dataset from provided path\n   261→        - Request body: { \"dataset_path\": \"/path/to/dataset\", \"iou_threshold\": 0.5 }\n   262→        - Response: { \"success\": true, \"dataset_id\": 1, \"total_images\": 100, \"total_classes\": 5, \"errors\": [] }\n   263→      - GET /api/dataset/metadata/:id: Get dataset metadata and summary statistics\n   264→      - DELETE /api/dataset/:id: Clear dataset from memory/database\n   265→    </dataset>\n   266→\n   267→    <statistics>\n   268→      - GET /api/statistics/:dataset_id: Get all per-class statistics\n   269→        - Response: { \"classes\": [...], \"overall_metrics\": {...}, \"iou_threshold\": 0.5 }\n   270→      - POST /api/statistics/recalculate: Recalculate metrics with new thresholds\n   271→        - Request body: { \"dataset_id\": 1, \"iou_threshold\": 0.6, \"confidence_threshold\": 0.7 }\n   272→        - Response: { \"success\": true, \"statistics\": {...} }\n   273→      - GET /api/statistics/export/:dataset_id: Export statistics to CSV/JSON\n   274→        - Query params: { \"format\": \"csv\" }\n   275→    </statistics>\n   276→\n   277→    <images>\n   278→      - GET /api/images/:dataset_id: Get list of all images with metadata (filename, thumbnail path, basic stats)\n   279→        - Query params: { \"page\": 1, \"per_page\": 20, \"class_filter\": \"car\", \"status_filter\": \"fp\" }\n   280→      - GET /api/images/:dataset_id/:image_id: Get detailed data for single image\n   281→        - Response: { \n   282→            \"filename\": \"img_001.jpg\", \n   283→            \"dimensions\": { \"width\": 1920, \"height\": 1080 },\n   284→            \"ground_truth_boxes\": [...],\n   285→            \"prediction_boxes\": [...],\n   286→            \"per_class_stats\": {...},\n   287→            \"thumbnail_path\": \"/static/thumbnails/img_001.jpg\"\n   288→          }\n   289→      - GET /api/images/thumbnail/:dataset_id/:filename: Serve generated thumbnail image\n   290→    </images>\n   291→\n   292→    <classes>\n   293→      - GET /api/classes/:dataset_id: Get list of all classes in dataset with counts\n   294→      - GET /api/classes/:dataset_id/:class_id: Get detailed statistics for single class\n   295→    </classes>\n   296→\n   297→    <health>\n   298→      - GET /api/health: Check server status and version\n   299→        - Response: { \"status\": \"healthy\", \"version\": \"1.0.0\", \"python_version\": \"3.9.7\", \"flask_version\": \"2.2.3\" }\n   300→    </health>\n   301→  </api_endpoints_summary>\n   302→\n   303→  <ui_layout>\n   304→    <main_structure>\n   305→      - User hovers over bounding boxes to see detailed info (IoU, confidence score)\n   479→      7. User uses previous/next buttons to navigate sequentially through images\n   480→    </key_interactions>\n   481→\n   482→  <implementation_steps>\n   483→    <step number=\"1\">\n   484→      <title>Project Setup and Environment Configuration</title>\n   485→      <tasks>\n   486→        - The application will process local datasets consisting of image sequences, ground truth bounding box JSON files, and model prediction JSON files (containing bounding boxes, classes, and confidence scores). It provides two core views: a statistics dashboard displaying per-class detection metrics (recall, false positive rate, etc.) and an image-by-image comparison view showing visual overlays of ground truth and predicted bounding boxes with distinct visual indicators for correct detections, false positives, and missed detections. The tool prioritizes intuitive visualization, accurate metric calculation, and seamless local file handling.\n  </overview>\n\n  <technology_stack>\n    <frontend>\n      <framework>Vanilla HTML5, CSS3, JavaScript (ES6+)</framework>\n      <styling>Custom CSS with Flexbox/Grid, optional Bootstrap 5 (via CDN) for responsive layout</styling>\n      <visualization>Chart.js (CDN) for statistical charts, Canvas API for bounding box rendering</visualization>\n      <file_handling>FileReader API for local file processing</file_handling>\n      <routing>Client-side routing with JavaScript (hash-based) for page navigation</routing>\n      <icons>Font Awesome (CDN) for visual indicators (check, cross, dash)</icons>\n    </frontend>\n    <backend>\n      <runtime>Python 3.8+</runtime>\n      <framework>Flask 2.0+</framework>\n      <data_processing>\n        - JSON parsing with built-in json module\n        - Image processing with Pillow (PIL) for thumbnail generation\n        - Metric calculation (recall, precision, FPR) with numpy\n      </data_processing>\n      <cors>Flask-CORS for cross-origin resource sharing</cors>\n      <file_management>Built-in os/pathlib for local file system interaction</file_management>\n    </backend>\n    <communication>\n      <api>RESTful endpoints for data processing and retrieval</api>\n      <data_format>JSON for all data exchange between frontend and backend</data_format>\n      <file_upload>Multipart/form-data for batch file upload (optional) or local file path specification</file_handling>\n    </communication>\n    <dependencies>\n      <python>\n        - flask>=2.0.0\n        - flask-cors>=3.0.10\n        - pillow>=9.0.0\n        - numpy>=1.21.0\n      </python>\n      <frontend_cdn>\n        - Chart.js v4.4.0\n        - Bootstrap 5.3.0 (optional)\n        - Font Awesome 6.4.0\n      </frontend_cdn>\n    </dependencies>\n  </technology_stack>\n\n  <prerequisites>\n    <environment_setup>\n      - Python 3.8+ installed on the system\n      - Flask and required dependencies installed via pip: pip install flask flask-cors pillow numpy\n      - Local dataset organized in a structured directory (images in /images, ground truth JSON in /gt, predictions JSON in /predictions)\n      - Backend code in /app directory with app.py as entry point\n      - Frontend assets (HTML/CSS/JS) in /app/static directory\n      - Template files in /app/templates directory\n      - Environment variables (optional) for dataset path configuration (.env file with DATASET_PATH)\n    </environment_setup>\n    <dataset_format>\n      <image_sequence>\n        - All images in a single directory (JPG/PNG format) with consistent naming convention (e.g., img_001.jpg, img_002.png)\n        - Image dimensions consistent or variable (tool should handle both)\n      </image_sequence>\n      <ground_truth_json>\n        - Single JSON file or per-image JSON files (naming matching images: img_001.json)\n        - Structure: {\n            \"filename\": \"img_001.jpg\",\n            \"width\": 1920,\n            \"height\": 1080,\n            \"annotations\": [\n              {\n                \"class\": \"car\",\n                \"bbox\": [x1, y1, x2, y2]  # pixel coordinates (top-left, bottom-right)\n              },\n              ...\n            ]\n          }\n      </ground_truth_json>\n      <prediction_json>\n        - Single JSON file or per-image JSON files (naming matching images: img_001_pred.json)\n        - Structure: {\n            \"filename\": \"img_001.jpg\",\n            \"width\": 1920,\n            \"height\": 1080,\n            \"predictions\": [\n              {\n                \"class\": \"car\",\n                \"bbox\": [x1, y1, x2, y2],\n                \"score\": 0.95  # confidence score (0-1)\n              },\n              ...\n            ]\n          }\n      </prediction_json>\n    </dataset_format>\n  </prerequisites>\n\n  <core_features>\n    <file_handling>\n      - Local dataset path configuration (input field for directory path)\n      - Validation of dataset structure (check for images, GT JSON, prediction JSON)\n      - Batch parsing of all files in the dataset directory\n      - Error handling for missing files, invalid JSON formats, and mismatched filenames\n      - Thumbnail generation for all images (150x150px, aspect ratio preserved)\n      - Caching of parsed data to avoid reprocessing on page refresh\n    </file_handling>\n\n    <statistics_dashboard>\n      <metrics_calculation>\n        - **Recall (True Positive Rate)**: TP / (TP + FN) per class\n        - **Precision**: TP / (TP + FP) per class\n        - **False Positive Rate (FPR)**: FP / (FP + TN) per class\n        - **F1 Score**: 2 * (Precision * Recall) / (Precision + Recall) per class\n        - **Overall Accuracy**: (TP + TN) / (TP + TN + FP + FN)\n        - **Average Precision (AP)** per class (optional)\n        - **Intersection over Union (IoU)** threshold configuration (default: 0.5) for TP/FP/FN classification\n      </metrics_calculation>\n      <visualization>\n        - Bar charts for per-class recall, precision, FPR\n        - Pie charts for class distribution in ground truth vs predictions\n        - Summary table with all metrics for easy comparison\n        - Sortable and filterable metric table (by class name, metric value)\n        - Export statistics to CSV/JSON format\n        - Interactive tooltips on charts showing exact metric values\n      </visualization>\n      <user_interface>\n        - Dropdown for IoU threshold adjustment (0.3 to 0.9 in 0.1 increments)\n        - Class filter (show/hide specific classes in charts/tables)\n        - Confidence score threshold filter for predictions (0.0 to 1.0 slider)\n        - Reset filters button to restore default settings\n        - Summary card with key overall metrics (total images, total classes, average recall/precision)\n      </user_interface>\n    </statistics_dashboard>\n\n    <image_comparison_view>\n      <left_panel>\n        - Searchable and filterable file list (by filename, class presence)\n        - Image thumbnails alongside filenames (150x150px)\n        - Scrollable list with fixed height (occupies 100% of viewport height)\n        - Highlight active/selected image in the list\n        - Pagination (optional) for large datasets (10/20/50 images per page)\n        - Class filter (show only images containing specific classes)\n        - Status filter (show only images with FP/FN/perfect detections)\n      </left_panel>\n      <right_panel>\n        <image_display>\n          - High-resolution image view (scaled to fit viewport, maintain aspect ratio)\n          - Interactive canvas overlay for bounding boxes\n          - Bounding box styles:\n            - True Positive (TP): Green border (2px), green checkmark (✓) at top-left corner\n            - False Positive (FP): Red border (2px), red cross (✗) at top-left corner\n            - False Negative (FN): Red border (2px), red horizontal dash (—) at top-left corner\n          - Bounding box labels (class name + confidence score for predictions)\n          - Zoom/pan functionality for detailed inspection\n          - Toggle visibility of ground truth/prediction boxes\n          - Toggle visibility of box labels/indicators\n        </image_display>\n        <per_image_statistics>\n          - Summary card for current image (filename, dimensions, total GT boxes, total predicted boxes)\n          - Per-class breakdown table (GT count, predicted count, TP, FP, FN for each class)\n          - IoU values for each matched bounding box (optional tooltip on hover)\n          - Confidence score distribution for predictions on current image\n          - Navigation buttons (previous/next image) for sequential viewing\n        </per_image_statistics>\n      </right_panel>\n    </image_comparison_view>\n\n    <navigation>\n      - Top navigation bar with links to Statistics Dashboard and Image Comparison View\n      - Active page indicator in navigation bar\n      - Breadcrumb navigation for context (current dataset path, current image)\n      - Back to top button for long pages (statistics dashboard)\n      - Responsive navigation (collapsible menu on mobile devices)\n    </navigation>\n\n    <error_handling>\n      - User-friendly error messages for invalid dataset paths\n      - Validation errors for malformed JSON files (line number + error description)\n      - Warning messages for mismatched filenames (GT/prediction JSON without corresponding image)\n      - Loading spinners during data processing/file parsing\n      - Empty state handling (no data loaded, no images to display)\n      - Fallback UI for unsupported image formats\n    </error_handling>\n\n    <accessibility>\n      - Keyboard navigation (Tab/Enter for list selection, arrow keys for image navigation)\n      - Alt text for all images and icons\n      - High contrast mode for bounding boxes (optional toggle)\n      - id (primary key, integer)\n        - path (text, unique)\n        - total_images (integer)\n        - total_classes (integer)\n        - iou_threshold (float, default 0.5)\n        - confidence_threshold (float, default 0.5)\n        - created_at (timestamp)\n        - last_updated (timestamp)\n      </dataset_metadata>\n\n      <image_metadata>\n        - id (primary key, integer)\n        - dataset_id (foreign key to dataset_metadata.id)\n        - has_fn (boolean)\n        - is_perfect (boolean)\n      </image_metadata>\n\n      <classes>\n        - id (primary key, integer)\n        - dataset_id (foreign key to dataset_metadata.id)\n        - name (text, unique per dataset)\n        - total_gt_count (integer)\n        - total_pred_count (integer)\n        - tp_count (integer)\n        - fp_count (integer)\n        - fn_count (integer)\n        - recall (float)\n        - precision (float)\n        - fpr (float)\n        - f1_score (float)\n      </classes>\n\n      <bounding_boxes>\n        - id (primary key, integer)\n        - image_id (foreign key to image_metadata.id)\n        - class_id (foreign key to classes.id)\n        - type (text, enum: 'ground_truth', 'prediction')\n        - x1 (float)\n        - y1 (float)\n        - x2 (float)\n        - y2 (float)\n        - confidence (float, null for ground truth)\n        - iou (float, null for unmatched boxes)\n        - classification (text, enum: 'tp', 'fp', 'fn', null for unclassified)\n      </bounding_boxes>\n    </tables>\n    <notes>\n      - Database is SQLite (file-based) for simplicity, stored as dataset_analysis.db\n      - Data is cleared/overwritten when a new dataset is loaded\n      - Indexes on filename, class name, and image_id for faster queries\n    </notes>\n  </database_schema>\n\n  <api_endpoints_summary>\n    <dataset>\n      - POST /api/dataset/load: Load and parse dataset from provided path\n        - Request body: { \"dataset_path\": \"/path/to/dataset\", \"iou_threshold\": 0.5 }\n        - Response: { \"success\": true, \"dataset_id\": 1, \"total_images\": 100, \"total_classes\": 5, \"errors\": [] }\n      - GET /api/dataset/metadata/:id: Get dataset metadata and summary statistics\n      - DELETE /api/dataset/:id: Clear dataset from memory/database\n    </dataset>\n\n    <statistics>\n      - GET /api/statistics/:dataset_id: Get all per-class statistics\n        - Response: { \"classes\": [...], \"overall_metrics\": {...}, \"iou_threshold\": 0.5 }\n      - POST /api/statistics/recalculate: Recalculate metrics with new thresholds\n        - Request body: { \"dataset_id\": 1, \"iou_threshold\": 0.6, \"confidence_threshold\": 0.7 }\n        - Response: { \"success\": true, \"statistics\": {...} }\n      - GET /api/statistics/export/:dataset_id: Export statistics to CSV/JSON\n        - Query params: { \"format\": \"csv\" }\n    </statistics>\n\n    <images>\n      - GET /api/images/:dataset_id: Get list of all images with metadata (filename, thumbnail path, basic stats)\n        - Query params: { \"page\": 1, \"per_page\": 20, \"class_filter\": \"car\", \"status_filter\": \"fp\" }\n      - GET /api/images/:dataset_id/:image_id: Get detailed data for single image\n        - Response: { \n            \"filename\": \"img_001.jpg\", \n            \"dimensions\": { \"width\": 1920, \"height\": 1080 },\n            \"ground_truth_boxes\": [...],\n            \"prediction_boxes\": [...],\n            \"per_class_stats\": {...},\n            \"thumbnail_path\": \"/static/thumbnails/img_001.jpg\"\n          }\n      - GET /api/images/thumbnail/:dataset_id/:filename: Serve generated thumbnail image\n    </images>\n\n    <classes>\n      - GET /api/classes/:dataset_id: Get list of all classes in dataset with counts\n      - GET /api/classes/:dataset_id/:class_id: Get detailed statistics for single class\n    </classes>\n\n    <health>\n      - GET /api/health: Check server status and version\n        - Response: { \"status\": \"healthy\", \"version\": \"1.0.0\", \"python_version\": \"3.9.7\", \"flask_version\": \"2.2.3\" }\n    </health>\n  </api_endpoints_summary>\n\n  <ui_layout>\n    <main_structure>\n      - {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"call_ae4c6fad4a3149c1b3d1cfb5","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→\"\"\"\n     2→Metrics calculation module for Image Detection Result Analyzer\n     3→Handles IoU calculation, bounding box matching, and metric calculations\n     4→\"\"\"\n     5→from typing import Tuple, List, Dict, Any, Optional\n     6→\n     7→\n     8→def calculate_iou(box1: Tuple[float, float, float, float],\n     9→                  box2: Tuple[float, float, float, float]) -> float:\n    10→    \"\"\"\n    11→    Calculate Intersection over Union (IoU) for two bounding boxes\n    12→\n    13→    Args:\n    14→        box1: First bounding box as (x1, y1, x2, y2) coordinates\n    15→        box2: Second bounding box as (x1, y1, x2, y2) coordinates\n    16→\n    17→    Returns:\n    18→        IoU value between 0.0 and 1.0\n    19→        - 1.0: Boxes perfectly overlap\n    20→        - 0.0: Boxes do not overlap\n    21→\n    22→    Note:\n    23→        Bounding box coordinates are in format (x1, y1, x2, y2) where:\n    24→        - (x1, y1) is top-left corner\n    25→        - (x2, y2) is bottom-right corner\n    26→    \"\"\"\n    27→    # Unpack box coordinates\n    28→    x1_min, y1_min, x1_max, y1_max = box1\n    29→    x2_min, y2_min, x2_max, y2_max = box2\n    30→\n    31→    # Calculate intersection coordinates\n    32→    intersection_x1 = max(x1_min, x2_min)\n    33→    intersection_y1 = max(y1_min, y2_min)\n    34→    intersection_x2 = min(x1_max, x2_max)\n    35→    intersection_y2 = min(y1_max, y2_max)\n    36→\n    37→    # Calculate intersection area\n    38→    intersection_width = max(0.0, intersection_x2 - intersection_x1)\n    39→    intersection_height = max(0.0, intersection_y2 - intersection_y1)\n    40→    intersection_area = intersection_width * intersection_height\n    41→\n    42→    # Calculate area of each box\n    43→    box1_area = (x1_max - x1_min) * (y1_max - y1_min)\n    44→    box2_area = (x2_max - x2_min) * (y2_max - y2_min)\n    45→\n    46→    # Calculate union area\n    47→    union_area = box1_area + box2_area - intersection_area\n    48→\n    49→    # Handle edge case where union is 0\n    50→    if union_area == 0:\n    51→        return 0.0\n    52→\n    53→    # Calculate IoU\n    54→    iou = intersection_area / union_area\n    55→\n    56→    return iou\n    57→\n    58→\n    59→def classify_bounding_boxes(gt_boxes: List[Tuple[float, float, float, float]],\n    60→                          pred_boxes: List[Tuple[float, float, float, float]],\n    61→                          iou_threshold: float = 0.5) -> Dict[str, List[Tuple]]:\n    62→    \"\"\"\n    63→    Classify bounding boxes as TP, FP, or FN based on IoU threshold\n    64→\n    65→    Args:\n    66→        gt_boxes: List of ground truth bounding boxes as (x1, y1, x2, y2) coordinates\n    67→        pred_boxes: List of prediction bounding boxes as (x1, y1, x2, y2) coordinates\n    68→        iou_threshold: IoU threshold for considering a prediction as TP (default: 0.5)\n    69→\n    70→    Returns:\n    71→        Dictionary containing:\n    72→        - tp: List of tuples (gt_index, pred_index) for true positives\n    73→        - fp: List of pred_index for false positives\n    74→        - fn: List of gt_index for false negatives\n    75→    \"\"\"\n    76→    # Track which boxes have been matched\n    77→    gt_matched = [False] * len(gt_boxes)\n    78→    pred_matched = [False] * len(pred_boxes)\n    79→\n    80→    # Find matches (TP)\n    81→    tp = []\n    82→    for pred_idx, pred_box in enumerate(pred_boxes):\n    83→        best_iou = 0.0\n    84→        best_gt_idx = -1\n    85→\n    86→        for gt_idx, gt_box in enumerate(gt_boxes):\n    87→            if gt_matched[gt_idx]:\n    88→                continue  # 1.0: Boxes perfectly overlap\n        - 0.0: Boxes do not overlap\n\n    Note:\n        Bounding box coordinates are in format (x1, y1, x2, y2) where:\n        - (x1, y1) is top-left corner\n        - (x2, y2) is bottom-right corner\n    \"\"\"\n    # Unpack box coordinates\n    x1_min, y1_min, x1_max, y1_max = box1\n    x2_min, y2_min, x2_max, y2_max = box2\n\n    # Calculate intersection coordinates\n    intersection_x1 = max(x1_min, x2_min)\n    intersection_y1 = max(y1_min, y2_min)\n    intersection_x2 = min(x1_max, x2_max)\n    intersection_y2 = min(y1_max, y2_max)\n\n    # Calculate intersection area\n    intersection_width = max(0.0, intersection_x2 - intersection_x1)\n    intersection_height = max(0.0, intersection_y2 - intersection_y1)\n    intersection_area = intersection_width * intersection_height\n\n    # Calculate area of each box\n    box1_area = (x1_max - x1_min) * (y1_max - y1_min)\n    box2_area = (x2_max - x2_min) * (y2_max - y2_min)\n\n    # Calculate union area\n    union_area = box1_area + box2_area - intersection_area\n\n    # Handle edge case where union is 0\n    if union_area == 0:\n        return 0.0\n\n    # Calculate IoU\n    iou = intersection_area / union_area\n\n    return iou\n\n\ndef classify_bounding_boxes(gt_boxes: List[Tuple[float, float, float, float]],\n                          pred_boxes: List[Tuple[float, float, float, float]],\n                          iou_threshold: float = 0.5) -> Dict[str, List[Tuple]]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Classify bounding boxes as TP, FP, or FN based on IoU threshold\n\n    Args:\n        gt_boxes: List of ground truth bounding boxes as (x1, y1, x2, y2) coordinates\n        pred_boxes: List of prediction bounding boxes as (x1, y1, x2, y2) coordinates\n        iou_threshold: IoU threshold for considering a prediction as TP (default: 0.5)\n\n    Returns:\n        Dictionary containing:\n        - recall: TP / (TP + FN)\n        - precision: TP / (TP + FP)\n        - fpr: FP / (FP + TN) [Note: TN is not available in object detection context]\n        - f1_score: 2 * (precision * recall) / (precision + recall)\n\n    Note:\n        FPR (False Positive Rate) in object detection context is typically calculated\n        as FP / (FP + TN), but TN (True Negatives) is often undefined or infinite\n        in object detection. Some implementations use FP / (FP + TP) or other metrics.\n        Here we calculate it as FP / (FP + TP) for simplicity.\n    \"\"\"\n    metrics = {}\n\n    # Calculate recall (True Positive Rate)\n    if (tp + fn) > 0:\n        metrics['recall'] = tp / (tp + fn)\n    else:\n        metrics['recall'] = 0.0\n\n    # Calculate precision\n    if (tp + fp) > 0:\n        metrics['precision'] = tp / (tp + fp)\n    else:\n        metrics['precision'] = 0.0\n\n    # Calculate FPR (False Positive Rate)\n    # In object detection, TN is often undefined. We use FP / (FP + TP) as an alternative\n    if (fp + tp) > 0:\n        metrics['fpr'] = fp / (fp + tp)\n    else:\n        metrics['fpr'] = 0.0\n\n    # Calculate F1 Score\n    if metrics['precision'] + metrics['recall'] > 0:\n        metrics['f1_score'] = 2 * (metrics['precision'] * metrics['recall']) / \\\n                             (metrics['precision'] + metrics['recall'])\n    else:\n        metrics['f1_score'] = 0.0\n\n    return metrics\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    import sys\n\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n    print(\"IoU Calculation Test\")\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n\n    #
